          <div class="t withAv">
           He considers metaphysics to be a waste of time. He doesn't value it because of it's lack of tangible use.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           I'm paraphrasing but his statements were along the lines of "while you're asking questions that can't be answered, I'm inventing new things" etc. etc.
           <br/>
           <br/>
           Obviously I'm bastardizing his quote and you should really find the exact quote if you want to get the real picture... but yeah, he's the kind of guy who is primarily concerned with the application of the intangible concept, not the pursuit of intangible concept with no intent of finding tangible applications for it.
          </div>
         </div>
        </div>

           <a href="http://new1.fjcdn.com/comments/Have+you+noticed+how+much+google+has+improved+recently+in+_712c4ddc20b3713e839da265fd253ade.png" rel="lightbox" style="white-space:normal;">
            <img alt="Have you noticed how much Google has improved recently in giving you the names of movies? For example, I watched &quot;Empire of the Sun&quot; recently, but had no idea what it was called. So, I searched, &quot;That movie about the kid in japan WWII&quot; and got the correct  title in the first result.   
   
Tried it with Bing, and not even close (though the answer was posted in a yahoo answers question to be fair). Bing, however, is awesome with porn while Google sucks now." class="av_img" original="http://new1.fjcdn.com/thumbnails/comments/Have+you+noticed+how+much+google+has+improved+recently+in+_712c4ddc20b3713e839da265fd253ade.png" src="http://new.fjcdn.com/site/funnyjunk/images/transparent_pixel.gif" style=" height:189px;"/>

          </div>
          Have you noticed how much Google has improved recently in giving you the names of movies? For example, I watched "Empire of the Sun" recently, but had no idea what it was called. So, I searched, "That movie about the kid in japan WWII" and got the correct  title in the first result.
          <br/>
          <br/>
          Tried it with Bing, and not even close (though the answer was posted in a yahoo answers question to be fair). Bing, however, is awesome with porn while Google sucks now.
         </div>
